  11.     private static int worker_num = 5;

  13.     private WorkThread[] workThrads;  
  14.     // æœªå¤„ç†çš„ä»»åŠ¡

  26.     private ThreadPool(int worker_num) {

  28.         workThrads = new WorkThread[worker_num];

  32.         }

  35.     // å•æ€æ¨¡å¼ï¼Œè·å¾—ä¸€ä¸ªé»˜è®¤çº¿ç¨‹ä¸ªæ•°çš„çº¿ç¨‹æ±   
  36.     public static ThreadPool getThreadPool() {

  40.     // å•æ€æ¨¡å¼ï¼Œè·å¾—ä¸€ä¸ªæŒ‡å®šçº¿ç¨‹ä¸ªæ•°çš„çº¿ç¨‹æ± ,worker_num(>0)ä¸ºçº¿ç¨‹æ± ä¸­å·¥ä½œçº¿ç¨‹çš„ä¸ªæ•°

  42.     public static ThreadPool getThreadPool(int worker_num1) {

  51.     public void execute(Runnable task) {

  54.             taskQueue.notify();  
  55.         }

  59.     public void execute(Runnable[] task) {

  62.                 taskQueue.add(t);

  68.     public void execute(List<Runnable> task) {

  71.                 taskQueue.add(t);

  77.     public void destroy() {  
  78.         while (!taskQueue.isEmpty()) {// å¦‚æœè¿˜æœ‰ä»»åŠ¡æ²¡æ‰§è¡Œå®Œæˆï¼Œå°±å…ˆç¡ä¼šå§

  83.             }

  85.         // å·¥ä½œçº¿ç¨‹åœæ­¢å·¥ä½œï¼Œä¸”ç½®ä¸ºnull  
  86.         for (int i = 0; i < worker_num; i++) {

  89.         }  
  90.         threadPool=null;  
  91.         taskQueue.clear();// æ¸…ç©ºä»»åŠ¡é˜Ÿåˆ—  
  92.     }  
  93.   
  94.     // è¿”å›å·¥ä½œçº¿ç¨‹çš„ä¸ªæ•°  
  95.     public int getWorkThreadNumber() {

  121.         private boolean isRunning = true;

  123.         / 
  124.           å…³é”®æ‰€åœ¨å•Šï¼Œå¦‚æœä»»åŠ¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸ç©ºï¼Œåˆ™å–å‡ºä»»åŠ¡æ‰§è¡Œï¼Œè‹¥ä»»åŠ¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ç©ºï¼Œåˆ™ç­‰å¾… 
  125.          */  
  126.         @Override  
  127.         public void run() {  
  128.             Runnable r = null;  
  129.             while (isRunning) {// æ³¨æ„ï¼Œè‹¥çº¿ç¨‹æ— æ•ˆåˆ™è‡ªç„¶ç»“æŸrunæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè¯¥çº¿ç¨‹å°±æ²¡ç”¨äº†  
  130.                 synchronized (taskQueue) {  
  131.                     while (isRunning && taskQueue.isEmpty()) {// é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸ºç©º  
  132.                         try {  
  133.                             taskQueue.wait(20);  
  134.                         } catch (InterruptedException e) {  
  135.                             e.printStackTrace();  
  136.                         }  
  137.                     }  
  138.                     if (!taskQueue.isEmpty())  
  139.                         r = taskQueue.remove(0);// å–å‡ºä»»åŠ¡  
  140.                 }  
  141.                 if (r != null) {  
  142.                     r.run();// æ‰§è¡Œä»»åŠ¡  
  143.                 }  
  144.                 finished_task++;  
  145.                 r = null;  
  146.             }  
  147.         }  
  148.   
  149.         // åœæ­¢å·¥ä½œï¼Œè®©è¯¥çº¿ç¨‹è‡ªç„¶æ‰§è¡Œå®Œrunæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè‡ªç„¶ç»“æŸ  
  150.         public void stopWorker() {  
  151.             isRunning = false;  
  152.         }  
  153.     }  
  154. }
